<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2003_Australian_Open" title="2003 Australian Open">2003 Australian Open</a></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Martina_Hingis" title="Martina Hingis">Martina Hingis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Anna_Kournikova" title="Anna Kournikova">Anna Kournikova</a> were the defending champions, but Hingis didn't participate in the tournament.<br/>
Kournikova partnered up with <a href="/wiki/Chanda_Rubin" title="Chanda Rubin">Chanda Rubin</a>, but they lost in the third round to <a href="/wiki/Conchita_Mart%C3%ADnez" title="Conchita Martínez">Conchita Martínez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nadia_Petrova" title="Nadia Petrova">Nadia Petrova</a>.<br/>
<a href="/wiki/Serena_Williams" title="Serena Williams">Serena Williams</a> and <a href="/wiki/Venus_Williams" title="Venus Williams">Venus Williams</a> won in the final 4–6, 6–4, 6–3, against <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Ruano_Pascual" title="Virginia Ruano Pascual">Virginia Ruano Pascual</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paola_Su%C3%A1rez" title="Paola Suárez">Paola Suárez</a>
</p>
